if (is_file('dev/test_database_plugins') && (sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') != '94a2f165700c7fe4113cdc58813c489c0616406c')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_database_plugins');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_database_plugins');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_database_plugins')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/test_database_plugins', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_database_plugins');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') != '94a2f165700c7fe4113cdc58813c489c0616406c') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_database_plugins', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_database_plugins');
}

if (is_file('dev/test_logmasks') && (sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') != 'd7c0c043b17bbf9cc738fdf3bbba3bdaf75f73bc')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_logmasks');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_logmasks');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_logmasks')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/test_logmasks', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('dev/test_logmasks')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_logmasks');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') != 'd7c0c043b17bbf9cc738fdf3bbba3bdaf75f73bc') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_logmasks');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_logmasks', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_logmasks');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '07b5b883f5934979323f436046b4430bd74e80e1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '07b5b883f5934979323f436046b4430bd74e80e1') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9922330d4b959d4a4a71616019e41d32829c000e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '07b5b883f5934979323f436046b4430bd74e80e1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'ef543702dd88210fdb895d8c444471ddbf4b1d69') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ef543702dd88210fdb895d8c444471ddbf4b1d69') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'fd6e7ef92a9eafd78bec9bec8b65f82e70d86e80') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ef543702dd88210fdb895d8c444471ddbf4b1d69') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'cba6f25f770d6fa002e28c1dce31dcd4d3a24456') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'cba6f25f770d6fa002e28c1dce31dcd4d3a24456') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '10c0eb96f936119f2e009062f4a0296e690344e3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'cba6f25f770d6fa002e28c1dce31dcd4d3a24456') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}
